# <a name="encryption-chains"></a><span data-ttu-id="a2c66-103">Chaînes de chiffrement</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="a2c66-103">Encryption chains</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="a2c66-104">Office 365 tire parti d’un certain nombre de fournisseurs de certificats.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="a2c66-104">Office 365 leverages a number of different certificate providers.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="a2c66-105">La liste complète des certificats racines Office 365 connus que les clients peuvent rencontrer lors de l’accès à Office 365 est décrite ci-dessous.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="a2c66-105">The following describes the complete list of known Office 365 root certificates that customers may encounter when accessing Office 365.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="a2c66-106">Pour plus d’informations sur les certificats que vous devrez peut-être installer dans votre propre infrastructure, voir [planifier les certificats SSL tiers pour Office 365](https://docs.microsoft.com/office365/enterprise/plan-for-third-party-ssl-certificates).</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="a2c66-106">For information on the certificates you may need to install in your own infrastructure, see [Plan for third-party SSL certificates for Office 365](https://docs.microsoft.com/office365/enterprise/plan-for-third-party-ssl-certificates).</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="a2c66-107">Les informations de certificat suivantes s’appliquent à toutes les instances mondiales et nationales de Cloud d’Office 365.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="a2c66-107">The following certificate information applies to all worldwide and national cloud instances of Office 365.</span></span>

>[!NOTE]
><span data-ttu-id="a2c66-108">Pour obtenir des informations sur les certificats qui s’appliquent aux clients **haute qualité DOD et GCC** , consultez la rubrique [chaînes de chiffrement Office 365-DOD et GCC High](encryption-office-365-certificate-chains-itar.md).</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="a2c66-108">For certificate information that applies to **DOD and GCC High** customers, see [Office 365 encryption chains - DOD and GCC High](encryption-office-365-certificate-chains-itar.md).</span></span>
